<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）会计估计对假设变化的敏感性；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）是否存在可以降低估计不确定性的经认可的计量技术</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">（</SPAN>当</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">然，作为输入数据的假设，其主观程度仍可导致估计不确定性</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）预测期的长度和从过去事项得出的数据对预测未来事项的相关性；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）是否能够从外部来源获得可靠数据；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN>）会计估计依据可观察到的或不可观察到的输入数据的程度。与会计估计相关的估计不确定性程度，可能影响会计估计对管理层偏向的敏感性。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 18.8pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.8pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>46</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">．在评估重大错报风险时，注册会计师考虑的事项也可能包括：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）会计估计的实际的或预期的重要程度；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）会计估计的记录金额（即管理层的点估计）与注册会计师预期应记录金额的差异；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）管理层在作出会计估计时是否利用专家工作；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）对上期会计估计进行复核的结果。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>（二）高度估计不确定性和特别风险</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>（参见本准则第十六条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>47</SPAN>．可能存在高度估计不确定性的会计估计举例如下：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）高度依赖判断的会计估计，如对未决诉讼的结果或未来现</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">金流量的金额和时间安排的判断，而未决诉讼的结果或未来现金流量</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">的金额和时间安排取决于多年后才能确定结果的不确定事项；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）未采用经认可的计量技术计算的会计估计；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）注册会计师对上期财务报表中类似会计估计进行复核的结</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">果表明最初会计估计与实际结果之间存在很大差异，在这种情况下管</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">理层作出的会计估计；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）采用高度专业化的、由被审计单位自主开发的模型，或在缺乏可观察到的输入数据的情况下作出的公允价值会计估计。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>48</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．由于存在估计不确定性，表面上不重要的会计估计同样可能</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">导致重大错报，即财务报表中确认或披露的会计估计金额的大小，可</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">能不能充分反映估计不确定性。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>49</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．在某些情况下，估计不确定性非常高，以致难以作出合理的</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">会计估计。因此，适用的财务报告编制基础可能禁止在财务报表中对此进行确认或以公允价值计量。在这种情况下，特别风险不仅与会计</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">估计是否应予确认或以公允价值计量相关，而且与披露的充分性相</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">关。针对这种会计估计，适用的财务报告编制基础可能要求披露会计</SPAN>估计和与之相关的高度估计不确定性（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">参见本指南第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>120</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt">段至第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>123</SPAN>段</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>50</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．如果认为会计估计导致特别风险，注册会计师需要了解与会</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">计估计相关的控制，包括控制活动。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>51</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．在某些情况下，会计估计的估计不确定性可能导致对被审计</SPAN>单位的持续经营能力产生重大疑虑。《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1324</SPAN>号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>持续经营》及其应用指南针对这种情况作出了规定并提供了指引。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">四、应对评估的重大错报风险</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>（参见本准则第十七条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.95pt">．《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>12</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>31</SPAN>号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">针对评估的重大错</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">报风险采取的应对措施》要求注册会计师设计和实施审计程序</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">包括</SPAN>其性质、时间安排和范围</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>，以应对与会计估计相关的评估的财务报</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">表层次和认定层次重大错报风险。本指南第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>53</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">段至第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>115</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">段重点说</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">明认定层次的具体应对措施。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>（一）对适用的财务报告编制基础要求的运用</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>（参见本准则第十<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑>七条第（一）项）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>53</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．许多财务报告编制基础规定会计估计的确认条件，并详细说</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">明作出会计估计的方法和需要作出的披露。这些规定可能较为复杂，</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">并要求运用判断。根据实施风险评估程序时了解的情况，注册会计师</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">需要重点关注适用的财务报告编制基础中容易被误用或产生不同解</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">释的相关要求。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>54</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．注册会计师确定管理层是否恰当地遵守适用的财务报告编制</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">基础的要求，在某种程度上依据其对被审计单位及其环境的了解。例</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">如，对某些项目</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（如在企业并购中获得的无形资产</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt">）</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">的公允价值进行</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">计量需要特别考虑被审计单位的性质及其经营活动的影响。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>55</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．在某些情况下，为了确定管理层是否恰当地遵守适用的财务</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">报告编制基础的要求，注册会计师有必要实施追加的审计程序，如检</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">查资产当前实物状况。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>56</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．在运用适用的财务报告编制基础的要求时，管理层需要考虑</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">影响被审计单位的环境或情况的变化。例如，特定类型资产或负债开</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">始引入活跃市场时，可能表明使用折现现金流量估计其公允价值不再恰当。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>（二</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LETTER-SPACING: -3.85pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>）</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>方法的一致性和变化的基础</SPAN></B></SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">参见本准则第十七条第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">二）</SPAN><FONT 
size=4>项）</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>57</SPAN>．在情况没有发生变化或没有出现新的信息时，对会计估计或估计方法作出改变是武断的。武断的变化导致各期财务报表不一致，并可能产生财务报表重大错报，或显示存在管理层偏向。因此，注册会计师考虑会计估计或其估计方法自上期以来发生的变化是非常重要的。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>58</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．管理层通常能够为不同期间基于环境的变化对会计估计或其</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">估计方法的改变提供很好的理由。注册会计师需要根据判断确定什么</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.9pt">构成很好的理由，以及该理由支持管理层观点</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">即环境已经发生变化，需要对会计估计或其估计方法作出改变</SPAN>）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">的充分性。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>（三）应对评估的重大错报风险</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>（参见本准则第十八条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>59</SPAN>．注册会计师在确定单独或综合运用本准则第十八条规定的措施以应对重大错报风险时，需要考虑下列事项的影响：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）会计估计的性质，包括会计估计是源于常规还是非常规交易；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）预期审计程序能否有效地为注册会计师提供充分、适当的审计证据；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）评估的重大错报风险，包括评估的风险是否是特别风险。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>60</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．例如，在评估坏账准备的合理性时，检查期后的现金回收情</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">况并结合其他程序可能是有效的审计程序。当与会计估计相关的估计</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">不确定性很高时，如会计估计是以采用不可观察到的输入数据的独有</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">模型为基础时，可能有必要综合运用本准则第十八条规定的应对措施</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">以获取充分、适当的审计证据。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>61</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt">．本指南第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>62</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt">段至第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>95</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">段为本准则第十八条规定的措施提供了进一步指引，解释每项应对措施可能适用的情况。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">截至审计报告日发生的事项</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">参见本准则第十八条第一款第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">一</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">）</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">项</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>62</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．如果截至审计报告日可能发生的事项预期发生并提供用以证</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">实或否定会计估计的审计证据，确定这些事项是否提供有关会计估计</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">的审计证据可能是恰当的应对措施。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>63</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．截至审计报告日发生的事项有时可能提供有关会计估计的充</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">分、适当的审计证据。例如，期后不久出售某被替代的产品的全部存</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">货，可能提供有关其可变现净值估计的审计证据。在这种情况下，如</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">果已获取有关该事项的充分、适当的审计证据，可能没有必要对会计</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">估计实施追加的审计程序。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>64</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．对于某些会计估计，截至审计报告日发生的事项不可能提供</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">审计证据。例如，与某些会计估计相关的情况或事项需要较长时间才有进展；同样，由于公允价值会计估计的计量目标，期后信息可能不</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">反映资产负债表日存在的事项或情况，因而可能与公允价值会计估计</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">的计量无关。本准则第十八条规定了注册会计师可能采取的应对重大</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">错报风险的其他措施。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>65</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．在某些情况下，与会计估计相矛盾的事项可能表明管理层没</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">有建立作出会计估计的有效流程，或者在作出会计估计时存在管理层偏向。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>66</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．即使决定对特定会计估计不采取这种方法，注册会计师仍需</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">要遵守《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1332</SPAN>号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">期后事项》及其应</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">用指南的相关规定。注册会计师需要实施审计程序，获取充分、适当</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">的审计证据，以确定财务报表日至审计报告日之间发生的、需要在财</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">务报表中调整或披露的事项是否已经按照适用的财务报告编制基础</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">在财务报表中得到恰当反映。由于除公允价值会计估计外的许多会计</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">估计的计量通常取决于未来情况、交易或事项的结果，《中国注册会</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">计师审计准则第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1332</SPAN>号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">期后事项》规定的审计工作对于这些会计估计尤为相关。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>对小型被审计单位的特殊考虑<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>67</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．当财务报表日和审计报告日相隔较长时，注册会计师对该期</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">间事项的复核可能是应对除公允价值会计估计外的其他会计估计的</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">有效措施。这对于某些业主亲自管理的小型被审计单位，特别是当管</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">理层没有针对会计估计建立正式的控制程序时尤其如此。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">测试管理层如何作出会计估计</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则第十八条第一款第</SPAN><FONT 
size=4>（二）项）</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>68</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．如果会计估计是依据模型</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">使用可观察到的或不可观察到的输入数据</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.55pt">）</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">作出的公允价值会计估计，测试管理层如何作出会计估计</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">和会计估计所依据的数据，可能是恰当的应对措施。此外，在下列情</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">况下，这种测试也可能是恰当的：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）会计估计源于被审计单位会计系统对数据的常规处理；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）注册会计师对上期财务报表中类似的会计估计的复核表明管理层本期的会计估计流程可能是有效的；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）会计估计建立在性质相似、单项不重要但数量众多的项目的基础上。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>69</SPAN>．测试管理层如何作出会计估计可能涉及下列方面，例如：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）测试会计估计所依据的数据的准确性、完整性和相关性，以及管理层是否使用这些数据和假设恰当地作出会计估计；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）考虑外部数据或信息的来源、相关性和可靠性，包括从管<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.8pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">理层聘请的、用以协助其作出会计估计的外部专家那里获取的数据或信息；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）重新计算会计估计，并复核有关会计估计信息的内在一致性；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）考虑管理层的复核和批准流程。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>对小型被审计单位的特殊考虑<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>70</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．在小型被审计单位，作出会计估计的流程的结构化程度相对</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">较低。管理层积极参与管理的小型被审计单位可能不存在对会计程序的全面描述、复杂的会计记录或书面政策。即使小型被审计单位没有</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">建立正式的流程，也并不意味着管理层不能为注册会计师测试会计估</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">计提供基础。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">评价计量方法</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则第十八条第一款第（二）项）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>71</SPAN>．当适用的财务报告编制基础没有规定计量方法时，评价计量方法（包括适用的模型）是否适用于具体情况属于职业判断。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>72</SPAN>．为了评价计量方法是否适用于具体情况，注册会计师可能需要考虑如下事项：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）管理层选择计量方法的理由是否合理；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）管理层是否充分评价和恰当运用适用的财务报告编制基础</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">提供的、用以支持所选择的计量方法的标准（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">如存在</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）根据被估计的资产或负债的性质和适用的财务报告编制基础的要求，评价计量方法是否适用于具体情况；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）计量方法相对于被审计单位开展的业务、所处行业和环境是否恰当。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>73</SPAN>．在某些情况下，管理层可能已确定采用不同的估计方法会导</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">致一系列显著不同的会计估计。在这种情况下，了解被审计单位如何</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">调查导致这些差异的原因可能有助于注册会计师评价管理层所选择</SPAN>方法的恰当性。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">评价模型的使用</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>74</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．在某些情况下，特别是作出公允价值会计估计时，管理层可</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.95pt">能使用模型。使用的模型是否适用于具体情况，可能取决于多种因素，</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt">如被审计单位的性质及其环境，包括被审计单位所处的行业和需要计</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">量的特定资产或负债。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>75</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．本指南第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>76</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">段所述事项的相关程度取决于具体情况，包括</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">模型是否公开出售供特定部门或行业使用，或是专有的模型。在某些</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">情况下，被审计单位可能利用专家来开发和测试模型。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>76</SPAN>．根据所处的不同环境，在测试模型时，注册会计师还可能考虑如下事项：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）在使用前是否验证模型，并定期复核以确保其能持续满足预定用途。被审计单位的验证流程可能包括：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
lang=EN-US>①</SPAN>评价模型理论上的合理性和数学上的可靠性，包括模型参数的恰当性；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
lang=EN-US>②</SPAN>评价模型输入数据相对于市场惯例的一致性和完整性；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
lang=EN-US>③</SPAN>与实际交易相比，评价模型的输出数据。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）是否存在针对模型变更的恰当控制政策和程序；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）是否定期校准和测试模型的有效性，特别是当输入数据具有主观性时；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）是否对模型输出数据作出调整，包括作出公允价值会计估计时，这些调整是否反映市场参与方在类似环境中所使用的假设；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）模型是否得到恰当记录，包括模型的预定用途、局限性和关键参数、要求的输入数据和实施验证分析的结果。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">管理层使用的假设</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则第十八条第一款第（二）项）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>77</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．注册会计师对管理层使用的假设的评价，仅以其在审计时可</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">获得的信息为基础。针对管理层假设而实施审计程序是为了财务报表</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">审计的目的，而不是为了针对假设本身发表意见。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>78</SPAN>．在评价管理层使用的假设的合理性时，注册会计师可能考虑诸如下列事项：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）单项假设是否显得合理；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）假设是否相互依赖且具有内在一致性；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）当将这些假设汇总起来考虑或结合其他假设考虑时，无论是对于特定会计估计还是其他会计估计，这些假设是否显得合理；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）对于公允价值会计估计，假设是否恰当地反映可观察到的市场假设。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>79</SPAN>．会计估计所依据的假设可能反映管理层对特定目标和战略结果的预期。注册会计师可以通过考虑假设是否与诸如下列事项相符，来实施审计程序评价这些假设的合理性：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）总体经济环境和被审计单位的经济情况；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）被审计单位的计划；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">以前期间所作的假设</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">如相关</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）被审计单位的经验或以前经历的情况（这种历史信息在一</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">定程度上可以代表未来情况或事项</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）管理层使用的与财务报表相关的其他假设。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>80</SPAN>．所使用的假设的合理性可能取决于管理层执行某项措施的意<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">图和能力。管理层通常记录与特定资产或负债相关的计划和意图，而</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">适用的财务报告编制基础可能也要求管理层作出这些记录。尽管所需获取的关于管理层意图和能力的审计证据的范围属于职业判断，注册</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">会计师实施的程序可能包括：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）复核管理层过去声称的意图的实现情况；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）复核书面计划和其他文档，包括得到正式批准的预算、授</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">权或会议纪要</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">如适用</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.05pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）向管理层询问执行某项措施的理由；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）复核财务报表日至审计报告日之间发生的事项；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）根据被审计单位面临的经济环境，评价其执行某项措施的能力，包括对现有承诺的影响。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">但是，某些适用的财务报告编制基础可能不允许在作出会计估计</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">时考虑管理层的意图或计划。作出公允价值会计估计通常不考虑管理</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">层的意图或计划，因为公允价值计量目标要求假设反映市场参与方可</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">能运用的假设。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>81</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．在评价管理层使用的构成公允价值会计估计基础的假设的合</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">理性时，注册会计师除了考虑本指南第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>78</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">段提及的事项外，在适用时还可能考虑下列事项：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）管理层是否以及如何在作出假设时加入特定市场输入数据（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">如相关</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）假设是否与可观察到的市场情况和以公允价值计量的资产或负债的特征一致；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）市场参与方假设的来源是否相关和可靠，以及当存在多种市场参与方假设时管理层如何选择假设；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）管理层是否以及如何考虑在可比较的交易、资产或负债中</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">使用的假设或有关信息</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">如适用</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>82</SPAN>．进一步讲，公允价值会计估计可能依据可观察到和不可观察到的输入数据。当公允价值会计估计依据不可观察到的输入数据时，注册会计师可能考虑的事项包括管理层是如何为下列方面提供合理支持的：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）识别与会计估计相关的市场参与方的特征；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）修改自有假设以反映市场参与方可能使用的假设；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）是否包括在具体情形下可获得的最佳信息；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">）</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">管理层的假设是如何考虑可比较的交易、资产或负债的</SPAN>（如适用</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.4pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">当存</SPAN>在不可观察到的输入数据时，注册会计师需要在评价假设时结合本准则第十八条提出的其他应对措施，以获取充分、适当的审计证据。在这种情况下，注册会计师有必要实施其他审计程序，如检查适当层级的管理层和治理层（如适用）复核和批准会计估计的文件。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>83</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．在评价支持会计估计的假设的合理性时，注册会计师可能识</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">别出一个或多个重大假设，这可能表明会计估计存在高度估计不确定</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.8pt">性并由此可能产生特别风险。本指南第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>102</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt">段至第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>115</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">段说明了应对</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">特别风险的其他措施。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">测试控制运行的有效性</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">参见本准则第十八条第一款第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">三</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -3.75pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">）</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">项）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>84</SPAN>．当管理层作出会计估计的流程的设计、执行和维护良好时，测试与管理层如何作出会计估计相关的控制运行的有效性可能是适当的。例如：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）存在适当层级的管理层和治理层（如适用）对会计估计进行复核和批准的控制；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）会计估计源于被审计单位会计系统对数据的常规处理。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>85</SPAN>．当存在下列情形之一时，注册会计师需要测试控制运行的有效性：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）在评估认定层次重大错报风险时，预期针对会计估计流程的控制的运行是有效的；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）仅实施实质性程序不能提供认定层次充分、适当的审计证据。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>对小型被审计单位的特殊考虑<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>86</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．小型被审计单位可能存在针对作出会计估计的控制，但其运</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">行的规范性存在差别。进一步讲，在管理层积极参与财务报告过程的</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.9pt">情况下，小型被审计单位可能确定某些类型的控制是不必要的。但是，</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">在极小型实体中，可能不存在太多注册会计师能够识别出的控制。因</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">此，注册会计师可能采用实质性方案应对重大错报风险，从而实施本</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">准则第十八条规定的一项或多项其他应对措施。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27.4pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">作出点估计或区间估计</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">参见本准则第十八条第一款第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（四</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -1.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">）项</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">和第二款</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>87</SPAN>．当存在诸如下列情形时，注册会计师作出点估计或区间估计以评价管理层的点估计，可能是恰当的应对措施：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）会计估计不是源于会计系统对数据的常规处理；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）注册会计师对管理层在上期财务报表中作出的类似事项的会计估计进行复核后认为本期流程不太可能是有效的；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）被审计单位没有恰当设计或执行针对会计估计流程的控制；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）财务报表日至审计报告日之间发生的事项或交易与管理层的点估计相互矛盾；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）注册会计师能够从其他来源获取作出点估计或区间估计时可使用的相关数据。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>88</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．即使被审计单位的控制得到恰当设计和执行，作出点估计或</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">区间估计也可能是应对已评估风险的有效</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">从效率或效果方面考虑</SPAN>）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">措施。在其他情况下，在确定是否有必要实施进一步审计程序及其性</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">质和范围时，注册会计师也可能考虑这种方法。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>89</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．注册会计师在作出点估计或区间估计时使用的方法可能有所</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">不同，取决于具体情况下哪种方法最有效。例如，注册会计师可能开</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">始时作出初始点估计，然后评估其对假设变化的敏感性，以确定用以评价管理层点估计的区间估计。在其他情况下，注册会计师可能首先</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">作出区间估计，然后再确定点估计</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">如可能</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>90</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．注册会计师作出点估计</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">相对于区间估计</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.2pt">）</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">的能力取决于许</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">多因素，包括使用的模型、可获得数据的性质和范围，以及会计估计</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">涉及的估计不确定性。进一步讲，作出点估计或区间估计的决定可能受到适用的财务报告编制基础的影响。该适用的财务报告编制基础可</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">能规定在考虑可供选择的结果和假设后所使用的点估计，或者规定特</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">定计量方法</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">如使用预期价值概率加权折现法</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>91</SPAN>．注册会计师可能采用诸如下列方法作出点估计或区间估计：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）使用模型，如公开出售供特定部门或行业使用的模型，或专有的模型，或注册会计师自行开发的模型；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）在管理层考虑可供选择的假设或结果的基础上进一步深入研究，如引入不同的一组假设；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）雇用或聘请在专门领域具有专长的人员开发或运用模型，或者提供相关假设；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）参照其他可比较的条件、交易或事项，或者可比较的资产</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">或负债的市场</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">如相关</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.05pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">了解管理层的假设或方法</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则第十八条第二款第（一）项）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>92</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．当注册会计师作出点估计或区间估计并使用有别于管理层的</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">假设或方法时，注册会计师需要按照本准则第十八条第二款第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN>一）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">项的要求充分了解管理层在作出会计估计时使用的假设或方法。这种</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">了解可能向注册会计师提供与其作出恰当点估计或区间估计相关的</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">信息，并有助于了解和评价任何有别于管理层点估计的重大差异。例</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">如，差异可能源于注册会计师与管理层使用不同但同样有效的假设。</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">这可能显示出会计估计对某些假设高度敏感，因此受高度估计不确定</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">性的影响，这意味着会计估计可能存在特别风险。此外，差异也可能是由于管理层造成的事实错误所导致。根据具体情况，注册会计师在</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">得出结论时，与管理层就使用的假设的基础及其有效性以及作出会计</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">估计的方法差异（</SPAN>如存在</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">）进行讨论可能是有帮助的。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">缩小区间估计</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则第十八条第二款第（二）项）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>93</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">．当注册会计师认为运用区间估计</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">注册会计师的区间估计</SPAN>）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">来评价管理层点估计的合理性是恰当的时，按照本准则第十八条第二</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1pt">款第</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">二</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.6pt">）</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">项要求作出的区间估计需要包括所有</SPAN></SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>合理</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">的结果而不是</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">所有可能的结果。这是因为包括所有可能结果的区间估计太宽泛以至</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">于不能有效地确定会计估计是否存在错报。如果注册会计师的区间估</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">计范围足够小以至于能够确定会计估计是否存在错报，它就是有用和有效的。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>94</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．通常情况下，当区间估计的区间已缩小至等于或低于实际执</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.9pt">行的重要性时，该区间估计对于评价管理层的点估计是适当的。但是，</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">对于某些特定行业，可能难以将区间缩小至低于某一金额。这并不必</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">然否定管理层对会计估计的确认，但是可能意味着与会计估计相关的</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt">估计不确定性可能导致特别风险。本指南第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>102</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.85pt">段至第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>115</SPAN>段说明了</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">应对特别风险的其他措施。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>95</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN
