style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．下列方法可以将区间估计的区间缩小至某一区域，使得在该</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">区域内的所有结果视为是合理的：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）从区间估计中剔除注册会计师认为不可能发生的极端结果；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）根据可获得的审计证据，继续缩小区间估计直至注册会计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">师认为该区间估计内的所有结果均视为是合理的。在极其特殊的情况</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">下，注册会计师可能缩小区间估计直至审计证据指向点估计。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>（四）考虑是否需要专门技能或知识</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>（参见本准则第十九条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>96</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．在计划审计工作时，注册会计师需要确定执行审计业务所需</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">资源的性质、时间安排和范围。这可能包括在必要时由具有专门技能</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">或知识的人员参与。此外</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1pt">，《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1121</SPAN>号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">对财务报表审计实施的质量管理》要求项目合伙人确信项目组和项目</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">组以外的专家整体上具有适当的胜任能力和必要素质。在审计会计估</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">计的过程中，注册会计师根据经验和业务的具体情况，可能认为需要</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">具备与会计估计的一个或多个方面相关的专门技能或知识。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 23.4pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>97</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">．当确定是否需要专门技能或知识时，注册会计师可能考虑的</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">事项包括：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）特定业务或行业中所涉及的资产、负债或所有者权益组成</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">部分的性质</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">如矿产储量、生物资产和复杂金融工具</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）高度的估计不确定性；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）涉及复杂计算或专门模型，如不存在可观察到的市场时估计公允价值；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）与会计估计相关的适用的财务报告编制基础的要求的复杂</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">性，包括是否存在容易产生不同解释的领域，或者会计实务不一致或</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">正在演变的领域；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）注册会计师拟采取的、应对评估的风险的审计程序。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>98</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">．对大多数会计估计，即使存在估计不确定性，也不太可能需</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">要专门技能或知识。例如，在评价坏账准备时，注册会计师不太可能</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">需要具备专门技能或知识。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>99</SPAN>．但是，当涉及会计或审计以外的领域时，注册会计师可能不</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">具备所要求的专门技能或知识，需要从专家那里获取有关技能或知</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.95pt">识。《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1421</SPAN>号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">利用专家的工作》及其</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">应用指南对确定雇用或聘请专家的必要性，以及当利用其工作时注册</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">会计师承担的责任作出了规定并提供了指引。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>100</SPAN>．在某些情况下，注册会计师可能认为有必要获取与会计或审计特定领域相关的专门技能或知识。具备这种专门技能或知识的人员可能为注册会计师所在的会计师事务所雇用，或者从外部机构聘请。如果这些人员对审计业务实施审计程序，从而成为项目组成员，相应地需要遵守《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1421</SPAN>号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>利用专家的工作》的规定。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>101</SPAN>．根据注册会计师对专家或具备专门技能或知识的人员的了</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">解以及与之交往的经验，注册会计师可能认为需要与所涉及的人员讨</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">论适用的财务报告编制基础的要求等事项，以确定其工作与审计目的</SPAN>相关。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">五、实施进一步实质性程序以应对特别风险</SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">参见本准则第二十条）</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>102</SPAN>．在审计导致特别风险的会计估计时，注册会计师在实施进一步实质性程序时需要重点评价下列事项：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）管理层是如何评估估计不确定性对会计估计的影响，以及这种不确定性对财务报表中会计估计的确认的恰当性可能产生的影响；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）相关披露的充分性。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑>（一）估计不确定性<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.8pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">管理层对估计不确定性的考虑</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">参见本准则第二十条第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">一</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -3.85pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">）</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">项）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>103</SPAN>．管理层可能根据具体情况采用多种方法评价会计估计的可</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">供选择的假设或结果。方法之一是敏感性分析，可能涉及确定会计估</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">计的金额如何随着假设的不同而变化。即使对于公允价值会计估计，</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt">由于不同市场参与方使用不同的假设，会计估计仍然可能存在差异。</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.2pt">敏感性分析可能针对</SPAN></SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>乐观</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>和</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>悲观</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">等不同情形得出一系列结果。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>104</SPAN>．敏感性分析结果可能表明会计估计对特定假设的变化不敏</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">感，也可能表明会计估计对一个或多个假设敏感，因而这些假设成为</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">注册会计师重点关注的对象。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>105</SPAN>．在处理估计不确定性时，某种特定方法（如敏感性分析）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">并不一定比其他方法更合适，管理层也并不一定需要通过细致的过程</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">和详尽的记录来体现对可供选择的假设或结果的考虑。重要的是管理层是否已评估了估计不确定性影响会计估计的方式，而不是所采用的</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.95pt">具体评估方法。相应地，当管理层没有考虑可供选择的假设或结果时，</SPAN>注册会计师有必要与管理层讨论其如何处理估计不确定性对会计估计的影响，并要求管理层提供支持性证据。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>对小型被审计单位的特殊考虑<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>106</SPAN>．小型被审计单位可能使用简单方法评估估计不确定性。除</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">复核可获得的文件外，通过询问管理层，注册会计师可能获取其他关</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">于管理层对可供选择的假设或结果进行考虑的审计证据。此外，管理层可能不具备考虑可供选择的结果或处理估计不确定性的专长。在这</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">种情况下，注册会计师可以向管理层解释处理估计不确定性的流程，</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">或其他可使用的不同评估方法，以及相应的记录。但是，这并不改变</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">管理层在财务报表编制方面承担的责任。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal">重大假设</B>（参见本准则第二十条第（二）项）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>107</SPAN>．如果在作出会计估计时运用的某些假设的合理变化可能对会计估计的计量产生重大影响，则这些假设被视为重大假设。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>108</SPAN>．从管理层建立的持续战略分析和风险管理流程中可能获得</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">相关信息，以支持管理层根据其了解的情况作出的重大假设。即使没</SPAN>有建立正式的流程</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">（</SPAN>如在小型被审计单位</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>，注册会计师可以通过询问管理层或与其讨论评价假设，并结合其他审计程序，获取充分、适</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">当的审计证据。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>109</SPAN>．本指南第</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>77</SPAN>段至第</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>83</SPAN>段描述了注册会计师在评价管理层作出的假设时需要考虑的事项。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">管理层的意图和能力</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则第二十条第（三）项）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>110</SPAN>．本指南第</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>13</SPAN>段和第</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>80</SPAN>段描述了注册会计师需要考虑的与管理层作出的假设及其意图和能力相关的事项。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>（二）作出区间估计</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>（参见本准则第二十一条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 25pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>111</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">．在编制财务报表时，管理层可能确信已经适当地处理了估</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">计不确定性对导致特别风险的会计估计的影响。但是，在某些情况下，</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">注册会计师可能认为管理层的工作是不够的，例如，注册会计师可能</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">作出以下判断：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）通过评价管理层如何处理估计不确定性的影响不能获取充分、适当的审计证据；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 21pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.25pt">）</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">有必要进一步分析与会计估计相关的估计不确定性的程度，</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">例如，注册会计师注意到类似环境下类似会计估计的结果存在较大差</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">别；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）不大可能通过如复核截至审计报告日发生的事项等审计程序获得其他审计证据；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）可能有迹象表明管理层在作出会计估计时存在管理层偏向。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>112</SPAN>．本指南第</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>87</SPAN>段至第</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>95</SPAN>段描述了在作出区间估计时注册会计师需要考虑的事项。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑'><FONT 
size=4>（三）确认和计量的标准<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">财务报表中对会计估计的确认</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则第二十二条第（一）项）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>113</SPAN>．如果管理层在财务报表中确认一项会计估计，注册会计师</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">评价的重点是会计估计的计量是否足够可靠，能否满足适用的财务报</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">告编制基础规定的确认标准。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>114</SPAN>．对于没有在财务报表中确认的会计估计，注册会计师评价</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">的重点是会计估计是否在实质上已满足适用的财务报告编制基础规</SPAN>定的确认标准。即使某一项会计估计没有得到确认，且注册会计师认</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">为这种处理是恰当的，可能仍然有必要在财务报表附注中披露具体情况。注册会计师也可能将被认为具有高度估计不确定性的会计估计确</SPAN>定为按照《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1504</SPAN>号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">在审计报告中沟</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.15pt">通关键审计事项》的规定，应当在审计报告中沟通的关键审计事项</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（如</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.1pt">适用</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>，注册会计师也可能认为有必要在审计报告中增加强调事项段<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>（参见《中国注册会计师审计准则第<SPAN lang=EN-US>1503</SPAN>号<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>——</SPAN>在审计报告中增加强调事项段和其他事项段》）。如果该事项被确定为关键审计事项，《中国注册会计师审计准则第<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1503</SPAN>号<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>——</SPAN>在审计报告中增加强调事项段和其他事项段》禁止注册会计师在审计报告中针对该事项增加强调事项段。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">会计估计的计量基础</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（参见本准则第二十二条第（二）项）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>115</SPAN>．对于公允价值会计估计，某些适用的财务报告编制基础在</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">要求或者允许进行公允价值计量和披露时，是以公允价值可以可靠计</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">量这一假定作为前提条件的。在某些情况下，如不存在恰当的计量方</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">法或基础，这种假定可能不成立。在这种情况下，注册会计师评价的</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">重点是管理层用以推翻适用的财务报告编制基础所规定的与采用公</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">允价值相关的假定的依据是否恰当。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.4pt"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.9pt; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">六、评价会计估计的合理性并确定错报</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（参见本准则第二十三条</SPAN>）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>116</SPAN>．根据获取的审计证据，注册会计师可能认为这些证据指向</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">与管理层的点估计不同的会计估计。当审计证据支持点估计时，注册</SPAN>会计师的点估计与管理层的点估计之间的差异构成错报。当注册会计</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">师认为使用其区间估计能够获取充分、适当的审计证据时，则在注册会计师区间估计之外的管理层的点估计得不到审计证据的支持。在这</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">种情况下，错报不小于管理层的点估计与注册会计师区间估计之间的</SPAN>最小差异。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>117</SPAN>．当管理层根据其对环境变化的主观判断而改变某项会计估</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">计，或者改变上期作出会计估计的方法时，基于获取的审计证据，注</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">册会计师可能认为会计估计被管理层随意改变而产生错报，或者将其</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">视为可能存在管理层偏向的迹象</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">参见本指南第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>124</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.9pt">段和第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>125</SPAN>段</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>118</SPAN>．针对注册会计师为了评价未更正错报对财务报表的影响而</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">如何区分错报</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.15pt">，《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1251</SPAN>号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">评价审计过</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">程中识别出的错报》及其应用指南作出了规定并提供了指引。一项错</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">报，无论是由于舞弊还是错误导致，当与会计估计相关时，可能是由</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">于下列因素导致的：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">毋庸臵疑地存在错报</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">事实错报</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）由注册会计师认为管理层对会计估计作出的判断不合理，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">或认为管理层对会计政策的选择或运用不恰当而产生的差异</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">判断错报</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）注册会计师对总体中错报的最佳估计，包括由审计样本中</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">识别出的错报推断出总体中的错报（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">推断错报</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT face=微软雅黑><FONT 
size=4>在某些涉及会计估计的情形中，错报可能由上述因素共同导致，因此难以或不可能区分出由哪一具体因素导致。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>119</SPAN>．评价在财务报表附注中的会计估计和相关披露</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">（</SPAN>无论是由</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">适用的财务报告编制基础要求的还是属于自愿披露的</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.7pt">）</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">的合理性时考</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">虑的事项，与在审计财务报表中确认的会计估计时考虑的事项在实质</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">上是相同的。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑"><FONT 
size=4>七、与会计估计相关的披露<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 26.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>（一</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>）</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style='FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: "Microsoft JhengHei",sans-serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt'>按照适用的财务报告编制基础作出的披露</SPAN></B></SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">参见本准则第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">二十四条</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt">）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>120</SPAN>．按照适用的财务报告编制基础列报财务报表，包括对重大</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">事项的充分披露。适用的财务报告编制基础可能允许或规定与会计估</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">计相关的披露，并且某些实体可能在财务报表附注中自愿披露额外信</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">息。例如，这些披露可能包括：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）使用的假设；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）使用的估计方法，包括适用的模型；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）选择估计方法的基础；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）改变上期估计方法产生的影响；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）估计不确定性的原因和影响。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 27.4pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt">这些披露与财务报表使用者理解在财务报表中确认或披露的会</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">计估计相关，注册会计师需要就其披露是否符合适用的财务报告编制</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">基础的规定获取充分、适当的审计证据。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>121</SPAN>．在某些情况下，适用的财务报告编制基础可能对披露估计不确定性作出特别规定。例如：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）披露关键假设以及产生估计不确定性的其他原因，该估计不确定性具有导致对资产和负债账面价值作出重大调整的特别风险。这些要求可能用</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>估计不确定性的关键原因</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>或</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>关键会计估计</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>等术语表述；<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）对于区间估计，披露可能出现的结果的区间和用以确定该区间的假设；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）披露关于公允价值会计估计相对被审计单位财务状况和经营成果的重要程度的信息；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）披露定性信息（如受风险影响的情况、被审计单位管理风险的目标、政策和程序以及计量风险的方法</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>，以及自上期以来这些<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>定性信息的任何变化；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）披露定量信息，如受风险影响的程度（以内部提供给关键</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">管理人员的信息为基础</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">，包括信用风险、流动性风险和市场风险。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT face=微软雅黑><FONT 
size=4>（二）披露导致特别风险的会计估计的估计不确定性（参见本准<B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4>则第二十五条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>122</SPAN>．对具有特别风险的会计估计，即使已按照适用的财务报告</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">编制基础的要求进行了披露，注册会计师仍可能根据所涉及的情况和</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">事实认为对估计不确定性的披露是不充分的。会计估计可能结果的区</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">间估计相对于重要性越大，注册会计师对估计不确定性的披露充分性</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">的评价越重要</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">参见本指南第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>94</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">段的相关讨论</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>123</SPAN>．在某些情况下，注册会计师可能认为鼓励管理层在财务报</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">表附注中描述与估计不确定性相关的情况是适当的。当注册会计师认为管理层在财务报表中对估计不确定性的披露不充分或存在误导时，</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.8pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1502</SPAN>号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">在审计报告中发表非无保</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">留意见》及其应用指南为注册会计师在这种情况下如何发表审计意见</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">作出了规定并提供了指引。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">八、可能存在管理层偏向的迹象</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>（参见本准则第二十六条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>124</SPAN>．在审计过程中，注册会计师可能注意到管理层作出的、可</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">能导致出现管理层偏向迹象的判断和决策。这些迹象可能影响注册会</SPAN>计师对有关风险评估结果和相关应对措施是否仍然恰当的判断，并且</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">注册会计师可能有必要考虑对审计其他方面的影响。进一步讲，这些</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">迹象可能影响注册会计师对财务报表整体是否不存在重大错报的评估（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.3pt">参见《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1501</SPAN>号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">对财务报表形成审计意见和出具审计报告》及其应用指南</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>125</SPAN>．与会计估计相关的、可能存在管理层偏向迹象的例子包括：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）管理层主观地认为环境已经发生变化，并相应地改变会计估计或估计方法；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）针对公允价值会计估计，被审计单位的自有假设与可观察到的市场假设不一致，但仍使用被审计单位的自有假设；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）管理层选择或作出重大假设以产生有利于管理层目标的点估计；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）选择带有乐观或悲观倾向的点估计。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">九、书面声明</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>（参见本准则第二十七条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US

style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">．《中国注册会计师审计准则第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>13</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>41</SPAN>号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN></SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">书面声明》及其</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">应用指南规范了书面声明的使用。根据估计不确定性的性质、重要性</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">和程度，有关财务报表中确认或披露的会计估计的书面声明可能包括</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">下列内容：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）计量流程（包括管理层在根据适用的财务报告编制基础作</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">出会计估计时使用的相关假设和模型</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.4pt">）</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">的恰当性，以及流程的一贯运用；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）假设恰当地反映了管理层代表被审计单位执行特定措施的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">意图和能力</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">当这些意图和能力与会计估计和披露相关时</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -6.9pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）在适用的财务报告编制基础下与会计估计相关的披露的完整性和适当性；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）不存在需要对财务报表中会计估计和披露作出调整的期后事项。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>127</SPAN>．针对未在财务报表中确认或披露的会计估计，书面声明也可能包括下列内容：<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）管理层用于确定不满足适用的财务报告编制基础规定的确</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">认或披露标准的依据的恰当性</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">参见本指南第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>段</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）针对未在财务报表中以公允价值计量或披露的会计估计，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">管理层用于推翻适用的财务报告编制基础规定的与使用公允价值相</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt">关的假定的依据的恰当性</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">（</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">参见本指南第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>115</SPAN>段</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><SPAN 
style="FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; mso-hansi-font-family: 微软雅黑">十、审计工作底稿</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>（参见本准则第二十八条）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>128</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">．在审计过程中，记录识别出的可能存在管理层偏向的迹象，</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.2pt">有助于注册会计师确定其风险评估结果和相关应对措施是否仍然恰</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">当，以及评价财务报表整体是否不存在重大错报。本指南第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>125</SPAN>段提</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">供了可能存在管理层偏向迹象的例子。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑>附录：（参见本指南第<SPAN 
lang=EN-US>1</SPAN>段）<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 28.6pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B 
style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 16pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt; mso-font-width: 95%">不同财务报告编制基础下公允价值的计量和披露</SPAN></B></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><B style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 16pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></B></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT face=微软雅黑><FONT 
size=4>本附录旨在讨论在不同财务报告编制基础下对公允价值的计量和披露。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>．不同的财务报告编制基础要求或允许在财务报表中作出不同</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">的公允价值计量和披露；同样，不同财务报告编制基础在提供关于资</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">产和负债计量或相关披露的指引上也存在差异。此外，某些特定行业</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">也存在公允价值计量和披露惯例。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>．不同财务报告编制基础之间，或者某一特定财务报告编制基</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.9pt">础中针对不同的资产、负债或披露，都可能存在不同的公允价值定义。</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.3pt">例如，《国际会计准则第</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>39</SPAN>号</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>——</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>金融工具：确认与计量》的公允价</FONT></SPAN><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">值定义为：在公平交易中，熟悉情况的自愿当事人之间交换资产或清</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">偿债务的金额。公允价值概念通常假设是当前交易而不是在过去或未来的某一日期进行结算。相应地，计量公允价值的流程可能是为了求</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.75pt">得交易发生时的估计价格。此外，不同的财务报告编制基础可能使用</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">不同的措辞，如</SPAN></SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>对特定实体的价值</FONT></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>、</FONT></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.25pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>在用价值</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">或类似术语，这些措辞均属于本准则中的公允价值概念。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>．财务报告编制基础可能采用不同方法处理因时间流逝而产生</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">的公允价值计量的变化。例如，某些财务报告编制基础可能要求将某些资产或负债的公允价值计量的变化直接在权益中反映，但在其他的</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">财务报告编制基础下可能反映在损益中。在某些财务报告编制基础</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">中，确定是否采用或如何应用公允价值会计受到管理层针对特定资产</SPAN>或负债执行某些措施的意图的影响。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>．不同财务报告编制基础可能要求在财务报表中采用某些特定</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">的公允价值计量和披露，以及详细规定或允许存在不同程度的计量和</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">披露。财务报告编制基础可能：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）对某些包含在财务报表中的信息、在财务报表附注中披露的信息或在补充资料中列报的信息规定计量与列报要求；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）允许被审计单位自行选择使用公允价值计量，或只有在满足特定条件时使用公允价值计量；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）规定确定公允价值的方法，如使用独立评估师，或详细规定采用折现现金流量的方法；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）允许在若干可替代方法中选择某种方法确定公允价值（财</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">务报告编制基础可能提供或没有提供选择标准</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7pt">）</SPAN>；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）除明显在行业惯例或会计实务中使用的公允价值计量方法和披露外，未提供任何指引。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><FONT size=4><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>．某些财务报告编制基础假定资产或负债的公允价值能够可靠</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">计量，并以此作为要求或允许采用公允价值计量或披露的前提条件。</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">在某些情况下，当资产或负债在活跃市场上不存在市场报价，并且其他合理估计公允价值的方法明显不恰当或不具有操作性时，这种假定</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">可能无法成立。某些财务报告编制基础可能详细规定确定公允价值的</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.7pt">层级框架，该框架将用于确定公允价值的输入数据分为下列两种极端</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">情况：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）清晰的</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>可观察到的输入数据</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>，这种输入数据基于公开报价和活跃市场；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-hansi-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）</SPAN></FONT><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>“</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>不可观察到的输入数据</FONT></SPAN><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style='FONT-FAMILY: "Times New Roman",serif; mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"; mso-ascii-font-family: 微软雅黑; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体'>”</SPAN><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>，这种输入数据涉及管理层自身<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑>关于市场参与方可能使用的假设的判断。<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN>．某些财务报告编制基础要求对估值信息作出某种明确的调整或修改，或者只针对某一特殊资产或负债进行特别考虑。例如，投资</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">性房地产的会计处理可能要求对所评估的市场价值进行调整，如销售</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">时的估计清理成本、房地产的状况和地理位臵以及其他事项。同样，</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">如果某一特殊资产不存在活跃市场，就可能要对公开市场报价进行调</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">整或修改，以形成对公允价值更加合理的计量。例如，如果市场交易</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">不频繁，市场发育不成熟，或者已发生的交易量相对于现有可供交易</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">的总量较小，则市场报价可能不代表公允价值。相应地，该市场价格</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">可能不得不作出调整或修改。在作出调整或修改时，可能有必要从其他渠道获取市场信息。进一步讲，在某些情况下</SPAN>（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">如当某种类型的债</SPAN>务投资有指定的担保物时</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -7.1pt">）</SPAN>，在确定一项资产或负债的公允价值或者</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">可能的资产减值时，可能有必要考虑相应的担保物。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>7</SPAN>．在绝大多数财务报告编制基础中，公允价值计量的前提是假</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">定企业是持续经营的，没有任何意图或必要进行清算，或者显著削减</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">经营规模，或者在不利条件下从事交易。因此，公允价值不是企业在强制性交易、非自愿性清算或强制清盘而收到或支付的金额。另一方面，总体经济环境或某些行业的特定经济状况可能导致市场缺乏流动性，并要求将萧条市场中的价格和潜在重大的萧条市场中的价格作为</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">公允价值的预测值。但是，在适用的财务报告编制基础规定或允许采</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">用公允价值计量，并且可能或没有规定如何计量的情况下，在确定资</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.65pt">产和负债的公允价值时，企业可能有必要考虑当前经济或经营形势的</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.4pt">影响。例如，管理层尽快处臵某项资产以满足特定经营目标的计划，</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">可能与确定该资产的公允价值相关。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 22.9pt"><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><FONT size=4><FONT face=微软雅黑><SPAN 
style="mso-font-width: 95%">公允价值计量的普遍性</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>8</SPAN>．公允价值的计量和披露在财务报告编制基础中逐渐得到广泛</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">使用。公允价值可能以多种方式在财务报表中出现，并影响财务报表</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">项目的确定，包括以公允价值计量下列项目：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>1</SPAN>）特定资产或负债，如有价证券或者某项金融工具项下的义务对应的负债，这些资产或负债需日常或定期采用市价计价；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>2</SPAN>）权益的特定组成部分。例如，对具有权益特征的某些金融工具（如可转换为普通股的可转换债券）进行确认、计量和列报；<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>3</SPAN>）在企业合并中获取的特定资产或负债。例如，企业合并中</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">购买一个企业而形成的商誉，通常以获取的可识别资产和负债的公允</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">价值以及给付对价的公允价值为基础；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>4</SPAN>）一次性调整为公允价值的特定资产或负债。一些财务报告</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">编制基础可能要求使用公允价值计量来量化一项资产或一组资产减</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.5pt">值的调整额。例如，在对企业合并中取得的商誉进行减值测试时，首</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">先确定明确界定的经营主体或报告单元的公允价值，再将该公允价值</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.6pt">分配至该经营主体或报告单元的资产或负债，以得出隐含商誉，最后</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.15pt">将隐含商誉与已记录商誉进行比较。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>5</SPAN>）资产和负债的汇总。在某些情况下，一类或一组资产或负</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt">债的计量需要将该类或该组的一些单项资产或负债的公允价值进行</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.55pt">汇总。例如，在适用的财务报告编制基础下，一项多样化的贷款组合</SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.35pt">的计量可能以构成该组合的一些贷款类型的公允价值为基础来确定。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></FONT></FONT></P>
<P class=af8 style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 24.2pt"><FONT size=4><FONT 
face=微软雅黑><SPAN style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685">（</SPAN><SPAN 
style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk94097685"><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style='mso-fareast-font-family: "Times New Roman"'>6</SPAN>）在财务报表附注中披露（或作为补充信息列报）未在财务报表中确认的信息。</SPAN></FONT></FONT><SPAN 
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P>
<P>&nbsp;</P>
<P></P></DIV>
